varying mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;

varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;

vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;

mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;

{

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;

    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);

    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);

    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;

    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;

uniform 	mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _DarkCorner;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainHighLightOffset;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;

varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;

    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);

    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_22 + u_xlat16_22;

    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_24 = (-u_xlat16_22) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat16_22 * u_xlat16_24;
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat16_24 * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_2 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_24);

    u_xlat16_3.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;

    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat16_22 * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat16_22 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_24 * u_xlat16_24 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_22 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_22;

    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_0.x + _MetallicOffset;

    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat5.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat23 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat23 = clamp(u_xlat23, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat26 = (-u_xlat0.x) * u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_24 * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat26;
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_24 / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat7;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat23) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat23) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat5.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat5.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;

    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat16_24 * 3.0;

    u_xlat16_1.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_27) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xzw;

    return;

    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);

    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;

    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_2 = texture2D(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat12 = (-u_xlat0.x) * u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat16_3.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat12;

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_1.x / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat18;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;

    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_3.xyz) * _ShadowColor1.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;

varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#ifdef FRAGMENT

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_3 = texture2D(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat10_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_9.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_9.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_5.z = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.y * u_xlat16_1.x + (-vs_TEXCOORD6.y);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, -0.100000001);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat10 = clamp(u_xlat10, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat26 = (-u_xlat10) * u_xlat10 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10 + u_xlat26;
    u_xlat10 = max(u_xlat10, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_1.x / u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat10 = min(u_xlat10, 100.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat10) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat6.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_5 = texture2D(_LightmapTex, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).wxyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat10_5.yzw;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat10_5.xxx + u_xlat2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_0.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat10_0.w * _IFEmiss + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_25 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _EmissColor.xyz + u_xlat2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ShadowColor1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * _ShadowColor1.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat10_5.x * u_xlat18 + -0.330000013;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat18 * u_xlat10_5.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * 3.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 * 3.0;
    u_xlat16_25 = clamp(u_xlat16_25, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * _ShadowColor2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ShadowColor2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz / u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);

#else
    precision mediump float;
#endif
precision highp int;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;

uniform 	mediump vec4 _ExposureColor;

uniform lowp sampler2D _BumpMap;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MixMap;
uniform lowp samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
vec3 u_xlat0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
float u_xlat23;
mediump float u_xlat16_24;
float u_xlat26;
mediump float u_xlat16_27;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_8.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_22 + u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_22)) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_24 = (-u_xlat16_22) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat16_22 * u_xlat16_24;
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat16_24 * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_2 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_24);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_2.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat16_22 * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat16_22 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_24 * u_xlat16_24 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_22 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_4 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _MainColor.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat5.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat23 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat23 = clamp(u_xlat23, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat26 = (-u_xlat0.x) * u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_24 * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat26;
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_24 / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat7;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat23) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat23) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat5.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat5.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat5.xyz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_0.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_8.x = sqrt(u_xlat10_0.z);
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat10_4.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_4.w + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw * _EmissColor.xyz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xzw * _ShadowColor1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xzw) * _ShadowColor1.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat23 + -0.330000013;
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat23 * 3.0;
    u_xlat16_27 = min(u_xlat16_27, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat16_24 * 3.0;
    u_xlat16_24 = clamp(u_xlat16_24, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_24) * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xzw) * _ShadowColor2.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw * _ShadowColor2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_27) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz / u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_1.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;

vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;

    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);

    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);

    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);

    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;

    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;

    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;

    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat12;

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_1.x / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat18;

    u_xlat0.xzw = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat0.xzw;

    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat0.xzw * _GISpecularColor.xyz;

    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;

vec4 u_xlat0;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;

    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);

    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;

    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);

    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;

    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.y * _HightMul + _HightOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat1.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;

    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);

    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;

    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;

    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;

out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;

vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;

mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_9.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_9.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_5.z = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.y * u_xlat16_1.x + (-vs_TEXCOORD6.y);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, -0.100000001);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat10 = min(max(u_xlat10, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat10 = clamp(u_xlat10, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat26 = (-u_xlat10) * u_xlat10 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10 + u_xlat26;
    u_xlat10 = max(u_xlat10, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_1.x / u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat10 = min(u_xlat10, 100.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat10) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat6.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_LightmapTex, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).wxyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_5.yzw;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx + u_xlat2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_0.w * _IFEmiss + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_25 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _EmissColor.xyz + u_xlat2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ShadowColor1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * _ShadowColor1.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat18 + -0.330000013;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat18 * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * 3.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_28 = min(max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 * 3.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_25 = min(max(u_xlat16_25, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_25 = clamp(u_xlat16_25, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * _ShadowColor2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ShadowColor2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;

    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    return;

    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);

    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;

    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;

    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);

    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;

    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat1.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxxx * vec4(u_xlat6);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;

    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.y * _HightMul + _HightOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat1.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxxx * vec4(u_xlat6);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

#endif

    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;

    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;

    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_6.w;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;

    u_xlat16_13.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_13.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_13.x = max(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0);

    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_13.x = exp2(u_xlat16_13.x);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_13.xxx;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_38 = min(max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

#endif
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat16_3.xzw) * _ShadowColor2.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xzw * _ShadowColor2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xzw;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;

    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;

    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;

    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);

    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;

    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);

    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;

    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);

    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;

    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxxx * vec4(u_xlat6);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;

    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.y * _HightMul + _HightOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat1.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxxx * vec4(u_xlat6);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;
    return;

    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;

    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat6.xyz;

    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;

    u_xlat7.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat7.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_31)) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = (-u_xlat16_13) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_13;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_1 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat10_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_13 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_13 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_13 = max(u_xlat16_13, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_13 = log2(u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_13 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_13 = exp2(u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_13 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_23) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat10_5.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_23 = sqrt(u_xlat10_5.z);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_13);

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_11.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_11.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + 1.0;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat10 = min(max(u_xlat10, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat10 = clamp(u_xlat10, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat20 = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat20 = min(max(u_xlat20, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat20 = clamp(u_xlat20, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

#else

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;

#else

    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;

    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x + u_xlat16_13.x;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * (-u_xlat16_13.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);

UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _GlobalLightEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _ShadowColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _ShadowColor2;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat0.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_0.y;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_0;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	mediump vec4 _GISpecularColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _GIDiffuseColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _ExposureColor;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _GlobalLightEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _ShadowColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _ShadowColor2;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _LightmapTex;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
bool u_xlatb2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat10;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_25;
float u_xlat26;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_9.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_9.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_5.z = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.y * u_xlat16_1.x + (-vs_TEXCOORD6.y);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, -0.100000001);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat10 = min(max(u_xlat10, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat10 = clamp(u_xlat10, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat26 = (-u_xlat10) * u_xlat10 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10 + u_xlat26;
    u_xlat10 = max(u_xlat10, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_1.x / u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat10 = min(u_xlat10, 100.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat10) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat6.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_LightmapTex, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).wxyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_5.yzw;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx + u_xlat2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w * _IFEmiss;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_0.w * _IFEmiss + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_25 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _EmissColor.xyz + u_xlat2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ShadowColor1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * _ShadowColor1.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat18 + -0.330000013;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat18 * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * 3.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_28 = min(max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 * 3.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_25 = min(max(u_xlat16_25, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_25 = clamp(u_xlat16_25, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * _ShadowColor2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ShadowColor2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz / u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    return;
}

 Pass {
  Name "ShadowCaster"
  LOD 300
  Tags { "IGNOREPROJECTOR" = "true" "LIGHTMODE" = "SHADOWCASTER" "QUEUE" = "Geometry" "RenderPipeline" = "LightweightPipeline" "RenderType" = "Opaque" }
  Cull Off
  GpuProgramID 110016
Program "vp" {
SubProgram "gles " {
"// hash: 7e1f6e5f7ab0171f
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowBias;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
uniform 	vec3 _LightDirection;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 100

#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
    precision highp float;
#else
    precision mediump float;
#endif
precision highp int;
#define SV_TARGET0 gl_FragData[0]
void main()
{
    SV_TARGET0 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

#endif
"

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}
